    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[BatchId], [p].[BatchNo], [p].[ProductId], [p0].[Name], [c].[Name] AS [Name0], [p0].[ModelNo], CASE
        WHEN [c0].[ColorId] IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
        ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
    END AS [c], [c0].[Name] AS [Name1], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [c1].[Name]
        FROM [ProductColor] AS [p1]
        INNER JOIN [Color] AS [c1] ON [p1].[ColorId] = [c1].[ColorId]
        WHERE [p0].[ProductId] = [p1].[ProductId]) AS [c0], [c0].[HexCode], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [c2].[HexCode]
        FROM [ProductColor] AS [p2]
        INNER JOIN [Color] AS [c2] ON [p2].[ColorId] = [c2].[ColorId]
        WHERE [p0].[ProductId] = [p2].[ProductId]) AS [c1], [p].[ProductionDate], [p].[Quantity], [p].[Status], [p].[CreatedAt], CAST((

        FROM [ProductItem] AS [p3]

        FROM [ProductItem] AS [p4]
        WHERE [p].[BatchId] = [p4].[BatchId] AND [p4].[PrintStatus] = N'Printed') AS bigint) AS [c3], CAST((
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [ProductItem] AS [p5]
        WHERE [p].[BatchId] = [p5].[BatchId] AND [p5].[Status] = N'Dispatched') AS bigint) AS [c4], [p0].[ProductId] AS [ProductId0]
    FROM [ProductionBatch] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Product] AS [p0] ON [p].[ProductId] = [p0].[ProductId]
    INNER JOIN [Category] AS [c] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [c].[CategoryId]
    LEFT JOIN [Color] AS [c0] ON [p].[ColorId] = [c0].[ColorId]
    WHERE [p].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_0 AND [p].[BatchId] = @__batchId_1
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[ProductId], [t1].[ColorId], [t1].[ColorId0], [t1].[CompanyId], [t1].[CreatedAt], [t1].[HexCode], [t1].[IsActive], [t1].[Name]
    FROM (
        SELECT [p6].[ProductId], [p6].[ColorId], [c3].[ColorId] AS [ColorId0], [c3].[CompanyId], [c3].[CreatedAt], [c3].[HexCode], [c3].[IsActive], [c3].[Name], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [p6].[ProductId] ORDER BY [p6].[ProductId], [p6].[ColorId], [c3].[ColorId]) AS [row]
        FROM [ProductColor] AS [p6]
        INNER JOIN [Color] AS [c3] ON [p6].[ColorId] = [c3].[ColorId]
    ) AS [t1]
    WHERE [t1].[row] <= 1
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ProductId0] = [t0].[ProductId]

    ) AS [t3]

) AS [t2] ON [t].[ProductId0] = [t2].[ProductId]
